(function() {
	let getCookie = function(cname) {
		let name = cname + "=";
		let decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
		let ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
		for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			let c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				c = c.substring(1);
			}
			if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
				return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			}
		}
		return "";
	}
	window.debugConsole = {
		log: function(...message) {
			if (getCookie("js-debug") === "true") {
				console.log(...message);
			}
		},
		debug: function(...message) {
			if (getCookie("js-debug") === "true") {
				console.debug(...message);
			}
		},
		error: function(...message) {
			if (getCookie("js-debug") === "true") {
				console.error(...message);
			}
		},
		info: function(...message) {
			if (getCookie("js-debug") === "true") {
				console.info(...message);
			}
		},
		warn: function(...message) {
			if (getCookie("js-debug") === "true") {
				console.warn(...message);
			}
		}
	}
})();

/**
 * Set the page's locale via a request_locale URL parameter. If there is already a URL parameter by
 * this name, then substitute it with the passed-in locale. NOTE: This function will actually cause the page
 * to be re-submitted with the new locale, so it really should not be used with pages submitted via POST
 * requests (if there are any, which I hope there are not).
 * @param locale the locale to set (e.g. en_US)
 */
function setPageLocale (locale) {
  var c=String (window.location);
  var rlpos = c.indexOf("request_locale=");
  var afterPart = "";
  if (rlpos > 0) {
    var afterBegin = c.indexOf("&", rlpos);
    if (afterBegin > 0) {
      afterPart = c.substring(afterBegin);
    }
    c = c.substring(0, rlpos-1);
  }
  var s=(c.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?');
  var np = c + s + 'request_locale=' + locale + afterPart;
  window.location = np;
}

function get_locale() {
  return "en_US";
}

function checkForPTMURL() {
	if ($j && $j.cookie && $j.cookie('PTM_URL')!=null
		&& window.location!=$j.cookie('PTM_URL')
		&& !window.location.href.match("/teachers/pw.html") ) {
			var path = $j.cookie('PTM_URL');
			$j.cookie('PTM_URL',null, { path: '/', expires: -1 });
			window.location.replace(path);
	}
}

        var isPdsuienabledCokkiesSet = $j.cookie('pdsuienabled');

            $j.cookie("pdsuienabled",isPdsPerfEnabled);

    }
}

function getEECProducts(){
    var isEcollectFormsEnabled = "1";
    var isEnrollmentExpressEnabled = "0";
    if (isEcollectFormsEnabled == "1" && isEnrollmentExpressEnabled == "1") {
        return "Enrollment Express, Ecollect Forms";
    } else if (isEcollectFormsEnabled == "1") {
        return "Ecollect Forms";
    } else if (isEnrollmentExpressEnabled == "1") {
        return "Enrollment Express";
    } else {
        return "";
    }
}


if(typeof pss_text!='function'){
function pss_text(key, params, returnKeyIfNotFound) {
	if (_messages[key] === undefined)
	{
		if (returnKeyIfNotFound !== undefined && returnKeyIfNotFound === true) {
			return key;
		} else {
			return "Message Key Was Not Found";
		}
	}
	if(params == null || params.length == 0)
	{
  		return _messages[key];
	}
	else
	{
		msg = _messages[key];
		for ( i = 0; i < params.length; i++)
		{
			token = "{"+i+"}";
			msg = msg.replace(token, params[i]);
		}
		return msg;
	}
}
}

function get_localized_date(d, fmt) {
   if (fmt === "mmdd") return ("" + ( (d.getMonth()+1) < 10 ? '0' + (d.getMonth() + 1) : (d.getMonth() + 1 ) ) + "/" + (d.getDate() < 10 ? '0' + d.getDate() : d.getDate() ) + "");
   return ("" + ( (d.getMonth()+1) < 10 ? '0' + (d.getMonth() + 1) : (d.getMonth() + 1 ) ) + "/" + (d.getDate() < 10 ? '0' + d.getDate() : d.getDate() ) + "/" + d.getFullYear() + "");
}


// Format is a formatting object
// number is number object
function formatNumber(format, number)
{
	var ds = format.ds; // decimal separator
	var result = "";

	if (isNaN(number) == true)
	{
		return number
	}
	else
	{
		result = number.toString();
		result = result.replace(".",ds);
		return result;
	}
}

function localizeNumber(number)
{
	return formatNumber(get_numeric_format(), number);
}

function deLocalizeNumber(number) {
	return removeNumberFormat(get_numeric_format(), number);
}

function removeNumberFormat(format, number) {
	// IE does not like instantiating RegExp objects with empty values, so we have to
	// check for valid values in the grouping separator before using it in a RegExp.
	var gsNotBlank = (format.gs == "." || format.gs == "," || format.gs == " ");
	number = number.toString();
	// We also want to check that only valid characters are present.
	var regexString = "^" + format.regex + "$";
	var validNumber = new RegExp(regexString, "g");
	if (number != "" && number.match(validNumber) != null) {
		if (gsNotBlank) {
			var gs = new RegExp("\\"+format.gs, "g");
			number = number.replace(gs, "")
		}
		var ds = new RegExp("\\"+format.ds, "g"); //The decimal separator is not expected to be empty
		number = parseFloat(number.replace(ds, "."));
	} else {
		return null;
	}
	return (isNaN(number)) ? null : number;
}

function localizeCurrency(number)
{
	return formatNumber(get_currency_format(), number);
}

<!-- This function return a json object with numeric formatting info -->
function get_numeric_format() {
   return  { format: '#,##0.#########', 
 size: '3', 
 gs: ',', 
 ds: '.', 
 regex: '([-]?(([0-9]{1,3}(,[0-9]{3})*(\\.[0-9]+)?|\\.[0-9]+)|([0-9]*(\\.[0-9]+)?)))' }; 
;
}

<!-- This function return a json object with currency formating info -->
function get_currency_format() {
   return  { format: '#,##0.00', 
 size: '3', 
 gs: ',', 
 ds: '.', 
 regex: '([-]?(([0-9]{1,3}(,[0-9]{3})*(\\.[0-9]+)?|\\.[0-9]+)|([0-9]*(\\.[0-9]+)?)))' }; 
;
}

if(!_messages) var _messages = {};
if(!_messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched) var _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched = [];
/**
 * Get texts from the server based on a prefix.
 * @param prefix the prefix to use
 * @param onlyIfNotPresent (optional) if passed, check to see if message is present yet; only fetch the
 *   texts from the server if this key is not present
 */
function pss_get_texts(prefix, onlyIfNotPresent) {
  if (onlyIfNotPresent && _messages[onlyIfNotPresent]) return;
  if (_messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched && _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched.includes(prefix.toLowerCase())) return;

  jQuery.ajax ({async: false,
    url:'/getMessages.action',
    data:{prefix: prefix, locale: get_locale()},
    dataType:'json',
    success: function (msgs) {
      jQuery.each(msgs, function (key, value) {
        _messages[key] = value;
      });
	  _messagePrefixesAlreadyFetched.push(prefix.toLowerCase());
    }
  });
}

//line breaks are 2 chracters on the backend (\r\n)
//IE treats them as 2 already but FF and Safari treat them
//as one (\n only). This will ensure all browsers are counting line
//breaks as 2
// This function is duplicated in muliple locations. Updating one requires
// updating all of them. They are located under
// web_root/wildcards/commonscripts.txt
// web_root/scripts/commonscripts.js
// sis/web/srv/views/psxdecorators/commonscripts.ftl
function realLength(str) {
	if (!str)
		return 0;

	//replace \r with empty string (this will only be matched on IE)
	var temp = str.replace(/\r/g, "");

	//find all occurances of newlines (\n)
	var lns = temp.match(/\n/g);

	if (lns)
		//if we had any newlines, do this hokie pokie to consistently count them as two
		return temp.length + lns.length;
	else
		//else no newlines, we can just use the strings actual length
		return str.length;
}


// trim function that truncates off the end of stringCopy until the string is less than
// maxlimit. Treats any new line (\n or \r\n) as two characters when trimmed
// off the end.
// stringCount should be calcuated by the function realLength. The value is either the
// length of stringCopy in chracters if isUnicode == false, or the length in bytes
// if isUnicode == true.
// This function is duplicated in muliple locations. Updating one requires
// updating all of them. They are located under
// web_root/wildcards/commonscripts.txt
// web_root/scripts/commonscripts.js
// sis/web/srv/views/psxdecorators/commonscripts.ftl
function trimToSize (stringCopy, stringCount, maxlimit, isUnicode) {

	var last_char;
	var secondToLast_char;
	var curval = stringCopy;
	var unicodeEscaped;
	var unicodeCharLength;
	for (; stringCount > maxlimit; ) {
		//get the last char in the string
		last_char = curval.charAt(curval.length-1);
		if (last_char == '\n') {
			//check if the second to last is a \r and yank that too
			secondToLast_char = curval.charAt(curval.length-2);

			if (secondToLast_char == '\r') {
				curval = curval.substring(0, curval.length-2);
			}
			else {
				curval = curval.substring(0, curval.length-1);
			}
			//line breaks need to be handled as 2 characters
			stringCount = stringCount - 2;
		}
		else {
			//character, pull it
			//figure out how many units to decriment the count by
			if (isUnicode) {
				unicodeEscaped = unescape( encodeURIComponent( last_char ) );
				unicodeCharLength = unicodeEscaped.length;
				stringCount = stringCount - unicodeCharLength;
			}
			else {
				stringCount = stringCount - 1;
			}


			curval = curval.substring(0, curval.length-1);
		}

	}
	// All done, field data is cut down to size. Save it.
	return curval;


}

// This function is duplicated in muliple locations. Updating one requires
// updating all of them. They are located under
// web_root/wildcards/commonscripts.txt
// web_root/scripts/commonscripts.js
// sis/web/srv/views/psxdecorators/commonscripts.ftl
function maxlength( field, maxlimit, leftCountSpan ) {
	var ret = true;
	var scrollDown = false;
	var characterCount = realLength(field.value);
	var stringCopy;
	var isUnicode;
	var hasChanged = false;

	// Check max field length. Now modified to also take Oracle 4000B limit into account.
    if ( characterCount > maxlimit ) {
      	stringCopy = field.value;
      	isUnicode = false;
      	field.value = trimToSize (stringCopy, characterCount, maxlimit, isUnicode);

		characterCount = realLength(field.value); //update the charCount since we've altered the string
        scrollDown = true;
        ret = false;
        hasChanged = true;
    }

    var utf8 = unescape( encodeURIComponent( field.value ) );
    var unicodeCharacterCount = realLength(utf8);
    if (unicodeCharacterCount > 4000) {
      stringCopy = field.value;
      isUnicode = true;
      var maxBytes = 4000;
      field.value = trimToSize(stringCopy, unicodeCharacterCount, maxBytes, isUnicode);

      characterCount = realLength(field.value); //update the charCount since we've altered the string
      utf8 = unescape( encodeURIComponent( field.value ) );
      unicodeCharacterCount = realLength(utf8); //update the unicodeCharCount since we've altered the string
      ret = false;
      scrollDown = true;
      hasChanged = true;
    }

    if (scrollDown) {
        field.scrollTop = field.scrollHeight;
    }

    // Find # left if caller wants to know
	if (leftCountSpan) {
	    var left1 = maxlimit - characterCount;
		var left2 = 4000 - unicodeCharacterCount;
		var left = (left1 < left2 ? left1 : left2);

		$j("#"+leftCountSpan).html(left);
    }

    if(hasChanged) {
        $j(field).trigger('change');
    }
    return ret;
}

function noNumbers(e) {
    var keynum, keychar, numcheck;
    if(window.event) keynum = e.keyCode; // IE
    else if(e.which) keynum = e.which; // Netscape/Firefox/Opera
    keychar = String.fromCharCode(keynum);
    numcheck = /\d/;
    return !numcheck.test(keychar);
}

function onlyNumbers(e) {
    return !noNumbers(e);
}

function decodeText(text) {
	return $j("<div/>").html(text).text();
}

var changeHistoryPayload = null;
/**
 * Creates the change history payload object if it doesn't already exist. Otherwise, it updates the existing object's context.
 */
function createOrUpdateChangeHistoryPayload(context) {
	if (changeHistoryPayload !== null) {
		changeHistoryPayload.context = context;
	} else {
	    changeHistoryPayload = {
	        context: context,
	        columns: []
	    };
	}
}

/**
 * Adds or replaces a key column on a payload object. If the table name and column match one that is already present,
 * the existing value is replaced.
 */
function setChangeHistoryColumn(tableName, columnName, value) {
	if (changeHistoryPayload !== null && tableName && columnName) {
		var list = changeHistoryPayload.columns;
		if (list && Array.isArray(list)) {
			var doAdd = true;
			for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
				var next = list[i];
				if (next.table_name.toUpperCase() === tableName.toUpperCase() && next.column_name.toUpperCase() == columnName.toUpperCase()) {
					next.column_value = value;
					doAdd = false;
					break;
				}
			}
			if (doAdd) {
				list.push({
					table_name: tableName,
					column_name: columnName,
					column_value: value
				});
			}
		}
	}
}

/**
 * Adds or replaces a set of options to be used to set a key column value. The column must first be created using setChangeHistoryColumn. Note that the column value will be made null.
 * tableName: The table name of the corresponding key column.
 * columnName: The column name of the corresponding key column.
 * label: The label to display in the UI for the select list. Localization should be done before passing in.
 * options: Array of options to display. Each object should have a name (for display) and value (for posting).
 * copyToColumns: Option array of arrays on which the selected value should be copied. Each array should have a column_name and column_value that corresponds to another key column.
 */
function addChangeHistoryColumnOptions(tableName, columnName, label, options, copyToColumns) {
	if (changeHistoryPayload !== null && tableName && columnName && options) {
		var list = changeHistoryPayload.columns;
		if (list && Array.isArray(list)) {
			for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
				var next = list[i];
				if (next.table_name.toUpperCase() === tableName.toUpperCase() && next.column_name.toUpperCase() == columnName.toUpperCase()) {
					next.column_value = null;
					next.column_option_label = label || columnName;
					next.column_options = options;
					next.copy_to_columns = copyToColumns;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		hideURLbar();
		adjustFrameStyles();

function adjustFrameStyles() {
	var containerFrame = document.querySelector('#container-frame');
	if (containerFrame && containerFrame.classList.contains('pds')) {
		var containerFrameMenu = document.querySelector('#container-frame-menu');
		if (containerFrameMenu) {
			document.body.classList.add('noScroll', 'backgroundAdjusted');
			var contentMain = document.querySelector('#content-main');
			if (contentMain) {
				contentMain.classList.add('autoScroll');
			}
		}
	}
}

function hideURLbar() {
	window.scrollTo(0,1);
	var appNav = document.querySelector('pds-app-nav');
	if (appNav) {
		document.getElementById('content-main').scrollTop = 0;
	}
}

//This function is used to convert the time string to the format HH:MM AM/PM
function convertTimeString(timeString) {
    if (timeString) {
        var timeParts = timeString.split(":");
        var hours = timeParts[0];
        if(timeParts[1] && timeParts[1].length > 2) {
            var minutes = timeParts[1].substring(0, 2);
            var meridiem = timeParts[1].substring(2).trim();
            var isPM = window.get_AMPM('pm');
            if (meridiem) {
                return hours + ':' + minutes + ' ' + (isPM === meridiem ? 'PM' : 'AM');
            } else {
                return timeString;
            }
        } else {
            return timeString;
        }
    }
}

<script>
// <input type="hidden" name="UF-009002320384" />
// <input type="hidden" name="UF-009002320385" />
var mbaRptCreatorAuth = mbaRptCreatorAuth || (() => {
    const opts = {
        api_domain: "ez.mba-link.com",
        plugin_name: "MBA Report Creator",
        pref_count_path: "/admin/mbaReportCreator/rcPrefs.json",
        status_name: "mba_rcStatus",
        exp_name: "mba_rcExpy",
        status: JSON.parse(`{"97":true,"98":true,"99":true,"888888":true,"999999":true,"1490001":true,"1490002":true,"1490003":true,"1490004":true,"1490008":true,"1490009":true,"1490011":true,"1490015":true,"1490016":true,"1490017":true,"1490018":true,"1490020":true,"1490022":true,"1490025":true,"1490027":true,"1490040":true,"1490045":true,"1490048":true,"1490049":true,"1490050":true,"1490053":true,"1490075":true,"1490080":true,"1490085":true,"1490090":true,"1490515":true,"1490525":true,"1490530":true,"1490531":true,"1490532":true,"1490533":true,"1490534":true,"1490535":true,"1490536":true,"1490537":true,"1490540":true,"1491538":true,"1492538":true,"1493538":true,"1494538":true,"1495538":true,"1496538":true,"1497538":true,"1498538":true,"1499990":true,"1499991":true,"1499992":true,"1499995":true,"1499997":true,"1499998":true,"1499999":true,"9999994":true,"9999995":true,"9999996":true,"9999997":true,"9999998":true,"14905371":true,"14905372":true,"authorized":true}` || null),
        exp: Number("1772132582502"),
        status_field: "UF-009002320384",
        exp_field: "UF-009002320385",
        old_prefs: {
            main: "1",
            schools: ""
        }
    }

    const CACHE_EXP = 30 * 60000; // 30 minutes
    const UNAUTH_CACHE_EXP = 1 * 60000; // 1 minute if not authorized
    const GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * 24 * 60 * 60000; // 14 days
    const TIMEOUT = 3000;

    async function checkEZApi() {
        return $j.ajax(`https://${opts.api_domain}/api/plugin/authCheck`, {
            timeout: TIMEOUT,
            data: { pluginName: opts.plugin_name },
            headers: { "X-Mba-DN": "01490000" }
        });
    }

    function checkOldPrefs() {
        if (opts.old_prefs.main == 1 && opts.old_prefs.schools) {
            return !opts.old_prefs.schools.includes("s0s");
        }
        return opts.old_prefs.main == 1;
    }

    async function updatePrefs(data) {
        if(typeof window[opts.status_name] !== 'undefined') return;
        window[opts.status_name] = true
        await $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', {
            "ac": "prim",
            [opts.status_field]: JSON.stringify(data),
            [opts.exp_field]: new Date().getTime() + (data.authorized ? CACHE_EXP : UNAUTH_CACHE_EXP),
        });
        cleanPrefs();
    }

    async function cleanPrefs() {
        const prefNames = {status: opts.status_name, exp: opts.exp_name};
        const prefIds = await $j.getJSON(opts.pref_count_path, prefNames);
        prefIds.pop();
        prefIds.forEach(deletePref);
    }

    function deletePref(recordId) {
        const pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        pass[`DR-009${recordId}`] = 'delete';
        $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', pass);
    }

    const isAuthed = d => d && d.authorized && ('0' == '0' || d['0']);
    return async function () {
        if (opts.exp && new Date().getTime() < opts.exp) {
            return isAuthed(opts.status);
        }

        if('admin' != 'admin') {
            return opts.status ? isAuthed(opts.status) : checkOldPrefs();
        }
        
        try {
            const apiResp = await checkEZApi();
            updatePrefs(apiResp);
            return isAuthed(apiResp);
        } catch (e) {
            if (e.status != 401 && opts.exp && new Date() < new Date(opts.exp + GRACE_PERIOD)) {
                return isAuthed(opts.status);
            }
            return e.status == 401 ? checkOldPrefs() : false;
        }
    }
})();

function mbaRcAuthAlert(){
    let msg = "The Report Creator Plugin has not been authorized.  Please contact MBA support for assistance.";
    psAlert({message:msg,title:'Plugin Not Authorized'});
    $j('.box-round, iframe').remove();
}

<script type="text/javascript">
	function mbaRcFindNavItem(itemId, startWith){
		if(typeof appNavItems == 'undefined') return;
		let items = startWith ? startWith.children || [] : appNavItems;
		let matchedItem;
		items.forEach(item => {	if (item.id == itemId) matchedItem = item;	});
		if(matchedItem)	return {"item":matchedItem,"parent":startWith ? startWith : appNavItems};
		//if not found, search children
		else{
			items.forEach(item => {	if(item.children && !matchedItem) matchedItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(itemId, item); });
			if(matchedItem) return matchedItem;
		}
	}

	//remove a link based on its id
	function mbaRcRemoveLink(linkId){
		let navItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.parent.children.splice(navItem.parent.children.indexOf(navItem.item),1);
	}

	//use this function to update the name or url property of a link
	function mbaRcUpdateLink(linkId, prop, value){
		let navItem = mbaRcFindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.item[prop] = value;
	}

    }else{
        //baDOS0 found so BA is on this server, don't send -1. Change to 0 for now
        baStatus = '0'
        baCid = '4212' || '';
        if(baCid) baStatus = baCid; //CID found, status is CID
    }

    const baCustomerJSON = `` || `{"partnerGUID":"8884CAED-188C-43A3-87EC-92E5977A7C93","adminLogin":"lnguyen@lawrence.k12.ma.us","adminUserPassword":"mba_ba_01490000","displayName":"Lawrence Public Schools","defaultCallerID":"9999999999","defaultAdminEmail":"lnguyen@lawrence.k12.ma.us","timeZoneCode":"CDT","iLicenseContactLimit":"13499","dtLicenseExpire":"12/31/1969","customerNumber":4212,"accessToken":"","prefJsName":"UF-009002328522"}`;
    let isBrightArrowClient = baStatus != '-1' && baStatus != '0' && baCustomerJSON.length < 5;
    return isBrightArrowClient;

		function mbaRcCheckUserAccess(){
			let mbaRcDevOnly = ['mbaRCconfigConfig','mbaRCfuncDev','mbaRCconfigCrsGrps','mbaRCconfigCredSums','mbaRCconfigCSS','mbaRCconfigJS','mbaRCconfigHistStand','mbaRCconfigImgs','mbaRCconfigCresSumDflts','mbaRCconfigGsMeters','mbaRCconfigModMgmt','mbaRCconfigTemplates','mbaRCTransCrs','mbaRCTransLangPref','mbaRCTransStandards','mbaRCTransTxt'];

<script>
  function HideStudentTransactionsSection() {
    if (!window.$j || !$j.fn) {
      window.setTimeout(HideStudentTransactionsSection, 50);
      return;
    }

    var $summary = $j('#navStudentTransactions');
    if (!$summary.length) {
      window.setTimeout(HideStudentTransactionsSection, 50);
      return;
    }

    var $li = $summary.closest('li');
    if ($li.length) {
      $li.remove();
      return;
    }

    var $details = $summary.closest('details');
    if ($details.length) {
      $details.remove();
    }
  }

  HideStudentTransactionsSection();
  $j(document).ready(HideStudentTransactionsSection);
</script>

var mbaAlertCreatorAuth = mbaAlertCreatorAuth || (() => {
    const opts = {
        api_domain: "ez.mba-link.com",
        plugin_name: "MBA Alert Creator",
        pref_count_path: "/admin/mbaAlerts/auth/checkAuthPrefs.json",
        status_name: "mba_alertCreatorStatus",
        exp_name: "mba_alertCreatorExp",
        status: JSON.parse(`{"97":true,"98":true,"99":true,"888888":true,"999999":true,"1490001":true,"1490002":true,"1490003":true,"1490004":true,"1490008":true,"1490009":true,"1490011":true,"1490015":true,"1490016":true,"1490017":true,"1490018":true,"1490020":true,"1490022":true,"1490025":true,"1490027":true,"1490040":true,"1490045":true,"1490048":true,"1490049":true,"1490050":true,"1490053":true,"1490075":true,"1490080":true,"1490085":true,"1490090":true,"1490515":true,"1490525":true,"1490530":true,"1490531":true,"1490532":true,"1490533":true,"1490534":true,"1490535":true,"1490536":true,"1490537":true,"1490540":true,"1491538":true,"1492538":true,"1493538":true,"1494538":true,"1495538":true,"1496538":true,"1497538":true,"1498538":true,"1499990":true,"1499991":true,"1499992":true,"1499995":true,"1499997":true,"1499998":true,"1499999":true,"9999994":true,"9999995":true,"9999996":true,"9999997":true,"9999998":true,"14905371":true,"14905372":true,"authorized":false}` || null),
        exp: Number("1772132582402"),
        status_field: "UF-009002315711",
        exp_field: "UF-009002315712",
        old_prefs: {
            main: "",
            schools: ""
        }
    }

    const CACHE_EXP = 30 * 60000; // 30 minutes
    const GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * 24 * 60 * 60000; // 14 days
    const TIMEOUT = 3000;

    async function checkEZApi() {
        return $j.ajax(`https://${opts.api_domain}/api/plugin/authCheck`, {
            timeout: TIMEOUT,
            data: { pluginName: opts.plugin_name },
            headers: { "X-Mba-DN": "01490000" }
        });
    }

    function checkOldPrefs() {
        if (opts.old_prefs.main == 1 && opts.old_prefs.schools) {
            return !opts.old_prefs.schools.includes("s0s");
        }
        return opts.old_prefs.main == 1;
    }

    async function updatePrefs(data) {
        if(typeof window[opts.status_name] !== 'undefined') return
        window[opts.status_name] = true
        await $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', {
            "ac": "prim",
            [opts.status_field]: JSON.stringify(data),
            [opts.exp_field]: new Date().getTime() + CACHE_EXP,
        });
        cleanPrefs()
    }

    async function cleanPrefs() {
        const prefNames = {status: opts.status_name, exp: opts.exp_name};
        const prefIds = await $j.getJSON(opts.pref_count_path, prefNames);
        prefIds.pop();
        prefIds.forEach(deletePref);
    }

    function deletePref(recordId) {
        const pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        pass[`DR-009${recordId}`] = 'delete';
        $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', pass);
    }
    let curSchoolId = ``;
    const isAuthed = d => d && d.authorized && (curSchoolId == 0 || d[curSchoolId]);
    return async function () {
        if (opts.exp && new Date().getTime() < opts.exp) {
            return isAuthed(opts.status);
        }

        if('admin' != 'admin') {
            return opts.status ? isAuthed(opts.status) : checkOldPrefs();
        }
        
        try {
            const apiResp = await checkEZApi();
            updatePrefs(apiResp);
            return isAuthed(apiResp);
        } catch (e) {
            if (e.status != 401 && opts.exp && new Date() < new Date(opts.exp + GRACE_PERIOD)) {
                return isAuthed(opts.status);
            }
            return e.status == 401 ? checkOldPrefs() : false;
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	let mbaAlertNav={};
	mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem = function(itemId, startWith){
		if(typeof appNavItems == 'undefined') return;
		let items = startWith ? startWith.children || [] : appNavItems;
		let matchedItem;
		items.forEach(item => {	if (item.id == itemId) matchedItem = item;	});
		if(matchedItem)	return {"item":matchedItem,"parent":startWith ? startWith : appNavItems};
		//if not found, search children
		else{
			items.forEach(item => {	if(item.children && !matchedItem) matchedItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(itemId, item); });
			if(matchedItem) return matchedItem;
		}
	}

	//remove a link based on its id
	mbaAlertNav.RemoveLink = function(linkId){
		let navItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.parent.children.splice(navItem.parent.children.indexOf(navItem.item),1);
	}

	//use this function to update the name or url property of a link
	mbaAlertNav.UpdateLink = function(linkId, prop, value){
		let navItem = mbaAlertNav.FindNavItem(linkId);
		if(!navItem) return;
		navItem.item[prop] = value;
	}
	mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed=function(){
		//Admin(main): top level leftnav links
		mbaAlertNav.RemoveLink('navMbaAlertCreator');

		//#Admin(student): leftnav links
		//replace selector with appropriate id.  This will remove a whole section
		$j('#navMbaAlertCreatorStudent').closest('.subcategory').remove();
	}

	$j(document).ready(function(){
	    //Authorization Check
	    try{
            mbaAlertCreatorAuth().then(isAuthorized=>{
                if(!isAuthorized){
            	    mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed();
            	}
    		});
    	}
    	//if plugin not installed or couldn't call the check (remove links)
    	catch (e){
    	    mbaAlertNav.AuthorizationFailed();
    	}
	});
</script></div>

        $j(window).load(function() {
            pageContext = 'Student';
            var gs = '';
            if((pageContext == 'Student' || pageContext == 'Staff') && gs=="true"){
                var links = document.body.getElementsByTagName('a');
                var len1 = links.length;
                for (var i=0; i<len1; i++) {
                    if(links[i].getAttribute('href') && !links[i].getAttribute('href').toLowerCase().includes('javascript')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('admin/contacts')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('/powerteacher')
                        && !links[i].getAttribute('href').includes('gs=true')
                        && links[i].getAttribute('href') !== '#') {
                        var url = new URL(links[i]);
                        url.searchParams.append('gs', true);
                        links[i].setAttribute('href',decodeURIComponent(url.href))
                    }
                }
                actionLinks = document.body.getElementsByTagName('form');
                var len2 = actionLinks.length;
                for (var i=0; i<len2; i++) {
                    if(actionLinks[i].action && !actionLinks[i].action.includes('gs=true')){
                        var acUrl = new URL(actionLinks[i].action);
                        acUrl.searchParams.append('gs', true);
                        actionLinks[i].setAttribute('action',decodeURIComponent(acUrl.href))
                    }
                }
            }
        })

<script>

//TODO: DO NOT WRITE CODE OUTSIDE OF THE FOLLOWING ANONYMOUS FUNCTION WITHIN THIS SCRIPT
(function() {
    //This is our appNavController. It's the ONE variable we are putting on the window in this file.  All other variables and functions used in this file need to be in this
    //JavaScript object to keep them off of the global namespace.
    window.appNavController = {
        frnOnPageLoad: '001215237',
        currentStudentFRN: '001215237',
        currentStaffFRN: '00557150',
        selectionInfo: {
            noOfStudentsInSelectionOnPageLoad: 1,
            firstStudentDcidInSectionOnPageLoad: '215237',
            noOfStaffsInSelectionOnPageLoad: 0,
            firstStaffDcidInSectionOnPageLoad: '0',
            pageContext: 'Student'
        },
        //This is called immediately after the definition of appNavController is complete.
        updateLastSelected: function() {
            var selectedDcid;
            if (/^[0-9]+$/.test(this.frnOnPageLoad)) {
                if (/^001/.test(this.frnOnPageLoad)) {
                    selectedDcid = this.frnOnPageLoad.slice(3);
                    localStorage.setItem('lastSelectedStudentDcid', selectedDcid);
                } else if(/^005/.test(this.frnOnPageLoad)) {
                    selectedDcid = this.frnOnPageLoad.slice(3);
                    localStorage.setItem('lastSelectedSchoolStaffDcid', selectedDcid);
                }
            } else {
                //This case was created for when the user changes schools which clears the current selection
                //and puts you back on the start page.
                if (this.selectionInfo.noOfStudentsInSelectionOnPageLoad <= 0) {
                    localStorage.removeItem('lastSelectedStudentDcid');
                }

                if (this.selectionInfo.noOfStaffsInSelectionOnPageLoad <= 0) {
                    localStorage.removeItem('lastSelectedSchoolStaffDcid');
                }
            }
        },
        getLastStudentSelected: function() {
            return localStorage.getItem('lastSelectedStudentDcid');
        },
        getLastStaffSelected: function() {
            return localStorage.getItem('lastSelectedSchoolStaffDcid');
        },
        replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl: function(currentUrl, frnValue) {
        var urlWithFrn = currentUrl;
        var frnStartIndex = urlWithFrn.indexOf('&frn=');
        if (frnStartIndex < 0) {
            frnStartIndex = urlWithFrn.indexOf('?frn=');
        }
        if (frnStartIndex >= 0) {
            // frn exists, replace it
            var frnEndIndex = urlWithFrn.indexOf('&', frnStartIndex + 1);
            if (frnEndIndex < 0) {
                urlWithFrn = urlWithFrn.substring(0, frnStartIndex + 5) + frnValue;
            } else {
                urlWithFrn = urlWithFrn.substring(0, frnStartIndex + 5) + frnValue + urlWithFrn.substring(frnEndIndex);
            }
        } else {
            // frn does not exist, append it
            var index = urlWithFrn.indexOf('?');
            if (index >= 0) {
                urlWithFrn = urlWithFrn + '&frn=' + frnValue;
            } else {
                urlWithFrn = urlWithFrn + '?frn=' + frnValue;
            }
        }
        return urlWithFrn;
        },
        clickOnStudentLink: function(navItem, event) {
            appNavController.clickOnStudentOrStaffLink(navItem, event, 'STUDENTS', false);
        },
        clickOnStaffLink: function(navItem, event) {
            appNavController.clickOnStudentOrStaffLink(navItem, event, 'STAFF', false);
        },
        clickOnStudentGroupFunctionLink: function(navItem, event) {
            appNavController.clickOnStudentOrStaffLink(navItem, event, 'STUDENTS', true);
        },
        clickOnStaffGroupFunctionLink: function(navItem, event) {
            appNavController.clickOnStudentOrStaffLink(navItem, event, 'STAFF', true);
        },
        clickOnContactGroupFunctionLink: function(navItem, event) {
            if(document.querySelector('pds-app-nav')){
                document.querySelector('pds-app-nav').setHighlights();
            }
            var currentContactSelectionTotal = document.getElementById('currentContactSelectionTotal') ? parseInt(document.getElementById('currentContactSelectionTotal').value) : null;
            if (currentContactSelectionTotal != null && currentContactSelectionTotal > 0) {
                redirectToContactsGroupFunction(navItem.url);
            } else {
                openPowerSearchDialog({enabled: true, modal: true, onlySearchType: 'contacts', url: navItem.url, isGroupFunctionModal: true, groupFunctionPageName: navItem.name});
            }
        },
        //This should be considered a private function. Call clickOnStudentLink or clickOnStaffLink.
        clickOnStudentOrStaffLink: function(navItem, event, studentOrStaff, isGroupFunction) {

            var tableNumber;                        //string
            var numberInSelectionOnPageLoad;        //number
            var firstDcidInSelectionOnPageLoad;     //string
            var searchType;                         //'students' | 'staff'
            var getLastStudentOrStaffSelected;      //function
            var firstDcidInSelectionElementId;      //string -> an html id
            var currentSelectionChangedElementId;   //string -> an html id
            var currentSelectionTotalElementId;     //string -> an html id
            var currentContext;                     //string

            switch(studentOrStaff) {
                case 'STUDENTS':
                    searchType = 'students';
                    tableNumber = '001';
                    getLastStudentOrStaffSelected = this.getLastStudentSelected.bind(this);
                    numberInSelectionOnPageLoad = appNavController.selectionInfo.noOfStudentsInSelectionOnPageLoad;
                    firstDcidInSelectionOnPageLoad = appNavController.selectionInfo.firstStudentDcidInSectionOnPageLoad;
                    firstDcidInSelectionElementId = 'firstStudentDcidInCurrentSelection';
                    currentSelectionChangedElementId = 'currentStudentSelectionChanged';
                    currentSelectionTotalElementId = 'currentStudentSelectionTotal';
                    currentContext = appNavController.selectionInfo.pageContext;
                break;
                case 'STAFF':
                    searchType = 'staff';
                    tableNumber = '005';
                    getLastStudentOrStaffSelected = this.getLastStaffSelected.bind(this);
                    numberInSelectionOnPageLoad = appNavController.selectionInfo.noOfStaffsInSelectionOnPageLoad;
                    firstDcidInSelectionOnPageLoad = appNavController.selectionInfo.firstStaffDcidInSectionOnPageLoad;
                    firstDcidInSelectionElementId = 'firstStaffDcidInCurrentSelection';
                    currentSelectionChangedElementId = 'currentStaffSelectionChanged';
                    currentSelectionTotalElementId = 'currentStaffSelectionTotal';
                    currentContext = appNavController.selectionInfo.pageContext;
                break;
            }

            if(document.querySelector('pds-app-nav')){
                document.querySelector('pds-app-nav').setHighlights();
            }
            var modifiedUrl = navItem.url;

            if (appNavController.frnOnPageLoad.startsWith(tableNumber)) {
                var dcidFromFrn = appNavController.frnOnPageLoad.substring(3);
                if (dcidFromFrn[0] !== '-') {
                    // positive dcid
                    if(numberInSelectionOnPageLoad == 0  && (isGroupFunction || currentContext == 'Normal')){
                        openPowerSearchDialog({enabled: true, modal: true, onlySearchType: searchType, url: modifiedUrl, isGroupFunctionModal: isGroupFunction, groupFunctionPageName: navItem.name});
                    }else{
                        if (!isGroupFunction){
                            modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(modifiedUrl, appNavController.frnOnPageLoad);
                        }
                        window.location.href = modifiedUrl;
                    }
                } else {
                    // negative student or staff dcid. can't use it. check if there is already a selection
                    if (numberInSelectionOnPageLoad > 0 ) {
                        if (!isGroupFunction) {
                            modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, tableNumber + firstDcidInSelectionOnPageLoad);
                        }
                        window.location.href = modifiedUrl;
                    } else {
                        modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, '???');
                        var redirctUrl = isGroupFunction ? navItem.url : modifiedUrl;
                        openPowerSearchDialog({enabled: true, modal: true, onlySearchType: searchType, url: redirctUrl, isGroupFunctionModal: isGroupFunction, groupFunctionPageName: navItem.name});
                    }
                }
                return;
            }

            //type: boolean
            var currentSelectionChanged =  document.getElementById(currentSelectionChangedElementId) && document.getElementById(currentSelectionChangedElementId).value === 'true';          
            if (currentSelectionChanged) {
                var currentSelectionTotal = document.getElementById(currentSelectionTotalElementId) ? parseInt(document.getElementById(currentSelectionTotalElementId).value) : 0;
                if (currentSelectionTotal > 0) {
                    var firstDcidInCurrentSelection = document.getElementById(firstDcidInSelectionElementId) ? document.getElementById(firstDcidInSelectionElementId).value : '0';
                    if (!isGroupFunction) {
                        modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, tableNumber + firstDcidInCurrentSelection);
                    }
                    window.location.href = modifiedUrl;
                } else {
                    modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, '???');
                    var redirctUrl = isGroupFunction ? navItem.url : modifiedUrl;
                    openPowerSearchDialog({enabled: true, modal: true, onlySearchType: searchType, url: redirctUrl, isGroupFunctionModal: isGroupFunction, groupFunctionPageName: navItem.name});
                }
            } else {
                lastUsedFrn = getLastStudentOrStaffSelected();
                if (lastUsedFrn != null) {
                    if (!isGroupFunction && !modifiedUrl.indexOf(studentOrStaff.toLowerCase() === 'students' ? appNavController.currentStudentFRN : appNavController.currentStaffFRN) < 0) {
                        modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, tableNumber + lastUsedFrn);
                    }
                    window.location.href = modifiedUrl;
                } else if (numberInSelectionOnPageLoad > 0) {
                    if (!isGroupFunction && 
                        ((studentOrStaff.toLowerCase() === 'students' ? !navItem.isInStudentSelection : !navItem.isInStaffSelection) || 
                        modifiedUrl.indexOf(studentOrStaff.toLowerCase() === 'students' ? appNavController.currentStudentFRN : appNavController.currentStaffFRN) < 0)) {
                        modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, tableNumber + firstDcidInSelectionOnPageLoad);
                    }
                    window.location.href = modifiedUrl;
                } else {
                    modifiedUrl = appNavController.replaceOrAppendFrnInUrl(navItem.url, '???');
                    var redirctUrl = isGroupFunction ? navItem.url : modifiedUrl;
                   openPowerSearchDialog({enabled: true, modal: true, onlySearchType: searchType, url: redirctUrl, isGroupFunctionModal: isGroupFunction, groupFunctionPageName: navItem.name});
                }
            }
        },
        //This is a function to open the url in a new tab
        openInNewTab: function(navItem, event){
            window.open(navItem.url, '_blank');
        },
        InitializeNav: function(){
            processNavItemTree(appNavItems);
            if(document.location.pathname.includes('/admin/contacts/edit.html') && document.location.href.includes('contactid=')) {
                setNewPageHighlightedRoute(appNavItems, '/admin/contacts/edit.html', '/admin/contacts/search.html?searchtype=contacts');
            }
            var appNav = document.querySelector('pds-app-nav');
            appNav.navigation = appNavItems;
            appNav.user = pdsUserName;
            appNav.userNavigation = pdsUserNavigation;
            if (typeof isMainNavChildPage !== 'undefined' && isMainNavChildPage) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    addBackButton();
                });

            }
        },
        InitializeNavforSearchTypeChange: function(oldSearchType, newSearchType){
            processNavItemTree(appNavItems);
            setNewPageHighlightedRoute(appNavItems, typeUrlMap.get(oldSearchType), typeUrlMap.get(newSearchType));
            var appNav = document.querySelector('pds-app-nav');
            appNav.navigation = appNavItems;
            appNav.user = pdsUserName;
            appNav.userNavigation = pdsUserNavigation;
            if (typeof appNav.setHighlights !== 'undefined'){
                appNav.setHighlights();
            }
        }
    };

    window.typeUrlMap= new Map([['students', '/admin/home.html?searchtype=students'], ['staff', '/admin/faculty/search.html?searchtype=staff'], ['contacts', '/admin/contacts/search.html?searchtype=contacts']]);
    
    function addBackButton () {
        if (document.getElementById('breadcrumbs') != null && document.getElementById('content-main')) {
            if (typeof backButtonText != 'undefined') {
                if (document.getElementById("backButton") != null) {
                    var prevPageBreadcrumb = document.getElementById("backButton");
                    if (prevPageBreadcrumb.querySelector('a')) {
                        if (prevPageBreadcrumb.querySelector('a').innerText.indexOf('[[placeholder]]') > -1) {
                            let innerText = prevPageBreadcrumb.querySelector('a').innerText.replace('[[placeholder]]', backButtonText);
                            prevPageBreadcrumb.querySelector('a').innerText = innerText;
                        }
                        document.getElementById('breadcrumbs').prepend(prevPageBreadcrumb);
                        if (prevPageBreadcrumb.classList.contains('concealed')) {
                            prevPageBreadcrumb.classList.remove('concealed');
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    var breadcrumbList = document.getElementById('breadcrumbs').querySelector('.breadcrumbs').querySelectorAll('a');
                    var prevPageBreadcrumb = breadcrumbList[breadcrumbList.length -1];
                    prevPageBreadcrumb.innerText = '< ' + backButtonText;
                    var newBreadcrumbContainer = document.createElement('div');
                    newBreadcrumbContainer.classList.add('back-button');
                    document.getElementById('breadcrumbs').prepend(newBreadcrumbContainer);
                    newBreadcrumbContainer.append(prevPageBreadcrumb);
                }
            }
        } else {
            setTimeout(() => {
                addBackButton();
            });
        }
    }

    //A recursive function that goes through all navItems and assigns the generic isCurrentRoute function to those that don't have one.
    //Removes any category items (items with no URL) that have no children
    function processNavItemTree (navItems) {
        let numberOfItems = 0;
        if (!(navItems instanceof Array)) {
            console.error('navItems needs to be an array.');
        }

        //looping through backwards so we can delete things
        for(var i=navItems.length-1; i>=0; i--) {
            numberOfItems++;
            var navItem = navItems[i];
            if (navItem.url != null) {
                var navItemUrl = navItem.url;
                var endIndex = navItem.url.indexOf('?');
                if(endIndex > 0) {
                    navItemUrl = navItemUrl.slice(0, endIndex);
                }
            }

        }
    }

    //Given appNavItems, the URL for the current route page in the left nav,  and the URL for a new page to highlight in the left nav
    //Remove the currentRoute function from the node with the current URL and put it on the new URL to make it the highlighted path
    //Note: document.querySelector('pds-app-nav').setHighlights(); may need to be called subsequently to see changes if InitializeNav() is being called manually
    function setNewPageHighlightedRoute (navItems, currentlyHighlightedPage, newHighlightedPage) {
        var navItemNodes = {
            "currentNode": undefined,
            "newNode": undefined
        };
        navItemNodes = getUrlNodesInNavItemsRecursive(navItems, currentlyHighlightedPage, newHighlightedPage, navItemNodes);
        if(navItemNodes.currentNode && navItemNodes.currentNode.isCurrentRoute) {
            var isCurrentRouteFunction = navItemNodes.currentNode.isCurrentRoute;
            navItemNodes.currentNode.isCurrentRoute = undefined;
            navItemNodes.newNode.isCurrentRoute = isCurrentRouteFunction;
        }
    }

    //Given a list of appNavItems, a currentUrl string, newUrl string, and a returnNodes js object with "currentNode" and "newNode" keys with undefined values
    //Return returnNodes js object with the appNav items/nodes that match their URLs if they exist
    function getUrlNodesInNavItemsRecursive(navItems, currentUrl, newUrl, returnNodes) {
        for(let item of navItems) {
            if(item.children) {
                returnNodes = getUrlNodesInNavItemsRecursive(item.children, currentUrl, newUrl, returnNodes);
                if(returnNodes.currentNode && returnNodes.newNode) {
                    return returnNodes;
                }
            } else if(item.url) {
                if(item.url.includes(currentUrl)) {
                    returnNodes.currentNode = item;
                    return returnNodes;
                } else if(item.url.includes(newUrl)) {
                    returnNodes.newNode = item;
                    return returnNodes;
                }
            }
        }
        return returnNodes;
    }

})();
</script>

<script>
// <input type="hidden" name="UF-009002315711" />
// <input type="hidden" name="UF-009002315712" />
var mbaAlertCreatorAuth = mbaAlertCreatorAuth || (() => {
    const opts = {
        api_domain: "ez.mba-link.com",
        plugin_name: "MBA Alert Creator",
        pref_count_path: "/admin/mbaAlerts/auth/checkAuthPrefs.json",
        status_name: "mba_alertCreatorStatus",
        exp_name: "mba_alertCreatorExp",
        status: JSON.parse(`{"97":true,"98":true,"99":true,"888888":true,"999999":true,"1490001":true,"1490002":true,"1490003":true,"1490004":true,"1490008":true,"1490009":true,"1490011":true,"1490015":true,"1490016":true,"1490017":true,"1490018":true,"1490020":true,"1490022":true,"1490025":true,"1490027":true,"1490040":true,"1490045":true,"1490048":true,"1490049":true,"1490050":true,"1490053":true,"1490075":true,"1490080":true,"1490085":true,"1490090":true,"1490515":true,"1490525":true,"1490530":true,"1490531":true,"1490532":true,"1490533":true,"1490534":true,"1490535":true,"1490536":true,"1490537":true,"1490540":true,"1491538":true,"1492538":true,"1493538":true,"1494538":true,"1495538":true,"1496538":true,"1497538":true,"1498538":true,"1499990":true,"1499991":true,"1499992":true,"1499995":true,"1499997":true,"1499998":true,"1499999":true,"9999994":true,"9999995":true,"9999996":true,"9999997":true,"9999998":true,"14905371":true,"14905372":true,"authorized":false}` || null),
        exp: Number("1772132582402"),
        status_field: "UF-009002315711",
        exp_field: "UF-009002315712",
        old_prefs: {
            main: "",
            schools: ""
        }
    }

    const CACHE_EXP = 30 * 60000; // 30 minutes
    const GRACE_PERIOD = 14 * 24 * 60 * 60000; // 14 days
    const TIMEOUT = 3000;

    async function checkEZApi() {
        return $j.ajax(`https://${opts.api_domain}/api/plugin/authCheck`, {
            timeout: TIMEOUT,
            data: { pluginName: opts.plugin_name },
            headers: { "X-Mba-DN": "01490000" }
        });
    }

    function checkOldPrefs() {
        if (opts.old_prefs.main == 1 && opts.old_prefs.schools) {
            return !opts.old_prefs.schools.includes("s0s");
        }
        return opts.old_prefs.main == 1;
    }

    async function updatePrefs(data) {
        if(typeof window[opts.status_name] !== 'undefined') return
        window[opts.status_name] = true
        await $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', {
            "ac": "prim",
            [opts.status_field]: JSON.stringify(data),
            [opts.exp_field]: new Date().getTime() + CACHE_EXP,
        });
        cleanPrefs()
    }

    async function cleanPrefs() {
        const prefNames = {status: opts.status_name, exp: opts.exp_name};
        const prefIds = await $j.getJSON(opts.pref_count_path, prefNames);
        prefIds.pop();
        prefIds.forEach(deletePref);
    }

    function deletePref(recordId) {
        const pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        pass[`DR-009${recordId}`] = 'delete';
        $j.post('/admin/changesrecorded.white.html', pass);
    }
    let curSchoolId = ``;
    const isAuthed = d => d && d.authorized && (curSchoolId == 0 || d[curSchoolId]);
    return async function () {
        if (opts.exp && new Date().getTime() < opts.exp) {
            return isAuthed(opts.status);
        }

        if('admin' != 'admin') {
            return opts.status ? isAuthed(opts.status) : checkOldPrefs();
        }
        
        try {
            const apiResp = await checkEZApi();
            updatePrefs(apiResp);
            return isAuthed(apiResp);
        } catch (e) {
            if (e.status != 401 && opts.exp && new Date() < new Date(opts.exp + GRACE_PERIOD)) {
                return isAuthed(opts.status);
            }
            return e.status == 401 ? checkOldPrefs() : false;
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var apiac = apiac || (function() {
    let API_FILES_PATH = "/admin/mbaAlerts/api/";
    switch ("admin") {
        case "teachers":
            API_FILES_PATH = "/teachers/mba_alerts/";
            break;
        case "subs":
            API_FILES_PATH = "/subs/mba_alerts/";
            break;
        case "guardian":
            API_FILES_PATH = "/guardian/mba_alerts/";
        default:
            break;
    }
    
    var API_QUERY_PATH = API_FILES_PATH+'queries/';
    var HAS_LOCALSTORAGE = (typeof(Storage) !== "undefined");
    var STORAGE_NAMESPACE = "mba.alertcreator.";

    // these fields will be stripped out of submit objects if found
    var NEVER_SUBMIT_FIELDS = [
        "whencreated",
        "whenmodified",
        "whocreated",
        "whomodified"
    ];
    var NO_FORMAT_FIELDS = [
        "frn",
        "students.dcid"
    ]
    
    // Simple submit function for use in api submits to a submitTo.txt page for
    function postData(data, customSubmit) {
         // do a small check to confirm we are in the admin portal

        // if a custom submit file was passed, submit there instead
        var submitToFile = customSubmit || 'submitTo.txt';
        return $j.post(API_FILES_PATH+'submit/'+submitToFile, data);

        
    }

    // Simple function to reduce repeated code in all of the getters
    function getData(filePath, passParams) {
        var defer = $j.Deferred();
        // if passParams is not already  object, make it an empty one
        if(typeof passParams !== 'object') passParams = {};
        $j.post(filePath, passParams, function(response) {
            // if it's an array, pop off the last element
            if(!!response && !!response.length) response.pop();
            defer.resolve(response);
        },'json').fail(function(res) {
            defer.reject({"error":"Network Failure", "response": res.responseText});
        });

        return defer;
    }

    function strReplaceAt(string, index, replacement) {
        return string.substr(0, index) + replacement + string.substr(index + replacement.length);
    }

    // creates a powerschool ready submit object to create a record
    function prepSubmit(table, obj) {
        var pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        var id = ('id' in obj && obj.id.length) ? obj.id : -99;
        obj = trimStringValues(obj)

        for(var key in obj){
            if(NEVER_SUBMIT_FIELDS.indexOf(key) > -1) continue
            
            if(NO_FORMAT_FIELDS.indexOf(key) > -1) {
                pass[key] = obj[key];
                continue
            }

            pass['CF-['+table+':'+id+']'+key] = obj[key];
        }
        return pass;
    }

    // Checks the object to see if it has all the properties in the given array
    function checkRequiredProperties(objToCheck, arrayOfProperties) {
        var missingProperties = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayOfProperties.length; i++) {
            var propertyToCheck = arrayOfProperties[i];
            if(objToCheck.hasOwnProperty(propertyToCheck) == false || objToCheck[propertyToCheck] === "") {
                missingProperties.push(propertyToCheck);
            }
        }
        return missingProperties;
    }

    // Trims all string values found in object
    function trimStringValues(obj) {
        for(var key in obj){
            if(typeof obj[key] === "string"){
                obj[key] = obj[key].trim();
            }
        }
        return obj;
    }

    //// PUBLIC FUNCTIONS
    var api = {};

        // Deletes given id record from given table
    api.deleteRecord = function(tableName, recordId) {
        var pass = {"ac":"prim"};
        pass['DD-'+tableName+'.id:'+recordId] = 1;
        return postData(pass);
    }

    api.saveAlert = function(obj) {
        var defer = $j.Deferred();

        if(obj.expiration) {
            obj.expiration = new Date(obj.expiration).toLocaleDateString("en-US")
        }

        var pass = prepSubmit('u_aet_customalerts', obj);
        postData(pass).then(function(response) {
            defer.resolve(response)
        }, function(response){
            defer.reject(response)
        })

        return defer;
    }
    //Advanced Trigger Directory Sync
    api.sync_adv_trigger_alerts = async function(){

    }

    //// GETTERS

    // gets the alert setup at the districts or schools, will always include alert set up at the district
    //   = comma delimited list of school number to limit alerts too
    //   = trigger type of the alert
    //   = 0 for enabled, 1 for disabled
    //   = 0 for enabled, 1 for disabled
    api.getAlertTypes = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getAlertTypes.json', p);
    }

    // gets the alert setup at the districts or schools, will always include alert set up at the district
    api.getAlerts = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getAlerts.json', p);
    }

    // gets the icon names for all the font awesome icons
    api.getFontAwesomeIcons = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'font-awesome.json', p);
    }

    // gets the user uploaded popups
    api.getUserPopups = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getUserPopups.json', p);
    }

    // gets user uploaded icons
    api.getUserIcons = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getUserIcons.json', p);
    }

    // gets user uploaded triggers
    api.getUserTriggers = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getUserTriggers.json', p);
    }

    // gets user uploaded triggers
    api.getUserGroups = function(p) {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getUserGroups.json', p);
    }

    api.getTriggeredManual = p => {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getTriggeredManual.json', p);
    }

    // gets students in section ids
    api.getStudentsInSection = function(p) {
        if(p && p.sectionIds && Array.isArray(p.sectionIds)) {
            p.sectionIds = p.sectionIds.map(Number).join(',');
        }
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getStudentsInSection.json', p);
    }

    api.getStudentsFieldValue = (p) => {
        return getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getStudentsFieldValue.json', p);
    }

    // gets the student fields available for student field value alerts
    api.getStudentFields = function(p) {
        let defer = $j.Deferred();
        let fieldsRetrieved = $j.Deferred();
        let fieldsNoLegacyRetrieved = $j.Deferred();
        let fieldList, noLegacyFieldList;
        // due to the comments required in the getStudentFields.json this will always return as rejected.
        //  need to strip out comments and then parse as json
        getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getStudentFields.json', p).then(null, function(response) {
            var resString = response.response.replace(/\/\*[\s\S]*?\*\/|([^\\:]|^)\/\/.*$/gm, "")
            resString = resString.split(' ').join('').split('\t').join('');
            try {
                fieldList = JSON.parse(resString);
                fieldsRetrieved.resolve();
            }catch(e) {
                defer.reject("unable to parse response");
            }
        });

        //this second call is necessary to get a list of fields that does not include legacy custom fields
        //we're still retrieving the original list in the old method (above) to ensure proper case for backwards compatibility
        getData(API_QUERY_PATH+'getStudentFieldsNoLegacy.json').then(function(response){
            response.pop();
            noLegacyFieldList = response;
            fieldsNoLegacyRetrieved.resolve();
        },function(){
            fieldsNoLegacyRetrieved.resolve();
        });

        $j.when(fieldsRetrieved, fieldsNoLegacyRetrieved).then(function(){
            //remove legacy custom fields from the list
            if(noLegacyFieldList) fieldList = fieldList.filter(f => noLegacyFieldList.includes(f.toLowerCase()));
            defer.resolve(fieldList);
        });
        return defer;
    }
    //Run a check to see if this file exists...
    api.UrlExists = (path)=>{
        result=false;
        $j.ajaxSetup({async:false});
        $j.get(path)
            .done(function(res) {result=res;})
            .fail(function() { result=false;})
        $j.ajaxSetup({async:true});
        return(result);
    }
    api.getAdvTriggerAlerts = (p) => {
        let path = API_QUERY_PATH+'getAdvTriggerMatches.html';
        if('querystring' in p && p.querystring.length) path += '?'+p.querystring;
        if('admin'=== 'subs'){ //advanced will not work on sub portal
            return false; 
        }//advanced student logic does not work across directories
        if('admin' == 'guardian'){
            path = `/guardian/alerts/user/triggers/${p.trigger_url}`;
            if(p.querystring) path += '?'+p.querystring;
            let curAlert = api.UrlExists(path);
            if(curAlert) return(JSON.parse(`{${curAlert}"-1": ""}`));
            else return false;
        }
        else{
            return getData(path, p);
        }
    }

    //// UTILITY FUCTIONS

    api.buildWhereClause = (operator, operand, fieldname) => {
        let operandIncludsNull = false;
        if(operand.length) {
            let operandArray = operand.split(",");
            operandArray = operandArray.map((e) => {
                e = e.trim()
                if(e.length == 0) operandIncludsNull = true;
                if(e[0] == '"') e = strReplaceAt(e, 0, "")
                if(e[e.length-1] == '"') e = strReplaceAt(e, e.length-1, "")
                return `'${e}'`
            })
            operand = operandArray.join(',')
        }
        switch (operator) {
            case "blank":
                 return"is null";
            case "in":
                if(operandIncludsNull) {
                    return`in (${operand}) or ${fieldname} is null`;
                } else {
                    return`in (${operand})`;
                }
            case "notin":
                if(operandIncludsNull) {
                    return`not in (${operand})`;
                } else {
                    return `not in (${operand}) or ${fieldname} is null`;
                }
        }
        
        return "is not null";
    }
    api.makeAlert = (obj) => {
        const requiredKeys = [
            "id",
            "stub_url",
            "studentdcid",
            "icon_type",
            "icon",
            "name",
            "color",
            "trigger_type",
            "sort_order",
            "school_number"
        ];
        for (const k of requiredKeys) {
            if(!(k in obj)) {
                console.error(`Can not make alert, missing required key: ${k}`);
                return
            }
        }

        let href = "";
        
        if(obj.stub_url!='') {
            let params={};
            if('admin'==='subs' || 'admin'==='guardian'){//subs & guardian cannot go cross portal
                params = {
                    url: obj.stub_url,
                    id: obj.id,
                    student_id: `${obj.studentid}`
                };
            }
            else{
                params = {
                    url: obj.stub_url,
                    frn: `001${obj.studentdcid}`,
                    id: obj.id,
                    student_id: `${obj.studentid}`
                };
            }            
            href = `/admin/alerts/aet_customalert_custompopup.html?${$j.param(params)}`
        } else {
            params={
                mba_frn: `001${obj.studentdcid}`,
                id: obj.id,
                student_id: obj.studentid
            };
            const linkMap = {
                "man": "aet_customalert",
                "sf": "aet_customalert_sf",
                "adv": "aet_customalert_adv"
            }
            href = `/admin/alerts/${linkMap[obj.trigger_type]}.html?${$j.param(params)}`
        }

        if(obj.trigger_type == "sf") {
            let sfParams={};
            if('admin'==='subs' || 'admin'==='guardian'){//subs & guardian cannot go cross portal
                sfParams = {
                    "mba_frn": `001${obj.studentdcid}`
                }
            }
            else{
                sfParams = {
                    "frn": `001${obj.studentdcid}`,
                    "mba_frn": `001${obj.studentdcid}`
                }
            }
            if(obj.student_field.indexOf('.') > -1) {
                sfParams["student_field"] = `${obj.ext_table_name}.`+obj.student_field.split('.')[1]
            } else {
                sfParams["student_field"] = obj.student_field
            }
            if(obj.ext_table_name != "") {
                sfParams["joinClause"] = `join ${obj.ext_table_name} on ${obj.ext_table_name}.studentsdcid = s.dcid`;
            }
            href += '&'+$j.param(sfParams);
        }

        if(obj.trigger_type == "adv") {
            href += '&'+obj.querystring;
            const otherParams = {
            };
            if('sectionid' in obj) {
                otherParams['sectionid'] = obj.sectionid;
            }
            if('studentid' in obj) {
                otherParams['studentid'] = obj.studentid;
//                otherParams['student_id'] = obj.studentid;
            }
            if('frn' in obj && 'admin'!=='subs' && 'admin'!=='guardian') {//subs & guardian cannot go cross portal
                otherParams['frn'] = obj.frn;
            }
            href += '&'+$j.param(otherParams);
        }
        
        var newalert = $j("<a>");
        newalert.addClass("dialogC");
        newalert.css('margin-left','4px');
        newalert.attr({
            href,
            title: obj.name,
            sort_order: obj.sort_order,
            school_number: obj.school_number,
            trigger_type: obj.trigger_type
        })
        newalert.html(api.makeAlertIcon(obj.icon_type, obj.name, obj.icon, obj.color))

        return newalert
    }
    
    api.makeAlertIcon = (iconType, name, icon, color) => {
        if(!iconType) return icon;

        let iconEl;
        switch (iconType) {
            case "fa":
                iconEl = $j('<i>');
                iconEl.addClass(icon);
                iconEl.addClass('mba-icon');
                iconEl.attr({
                    title: name
                });
                iconEl.css({
                    color: color/*,
                    "font-size": "20px"*/
                })
                break;

            case "u":
                iconEl = $j('<img>');
                iconEl.attr({
                    src: `/images/aet_customalerts/user/${icon}`
                })
                iconEl.addClass('mba-icon');
                if(icon.indexOf('.svg')>0){
                    /*
                    iconEl.css({
                        "max-height":"20px",
                        "max-width": "20px",
                        "font-size": "20px",                        
                        "width": "25px"
                    });
                    */
                }else{
                    /*
                    iconEl.css({
                        "max-height":"20px",
                        "max-width": "20px",
                        "font-size": "20px",                        
                        "width": "25px"
                    });
                    */
                }
                
                break;
        }
        return iconEl ? iconEl[0].outerHTML : icon;
    }
    
    /**
     * Takes json data and exports it out to a csv file.
     */
    api.exportData = function(fileName, exportData) {

        // this function only takes string data atm. may change later
        if(typeof exportData !== 'string') return;

        //download
        if(window.navigator.msSaveBlob){
            //IE version
            var blob = new Blob([exportData],{ type: "application/csv;charset=utf-8;"});
            navigator.msSaveBlob(blob, fileName);
        }else{
            //Chrome & FF
            var encodedUri = encodeURI("data:attachment/csv," + exportData);
            encodedUri = encodedUri.replace(/#/g, '%23');// FF does not encode '#', manually encode here
            var link = document.createElement('a');
            link.setAttribute("href", encodedUri);
            link.setAttribute("download", fileName);
            document.body.appendChild(link);
            link.click();
            $j(link).remove();
        }
    }

    // Sets the users current selection based on given dcids
    api.setCurrentSelection = function(dcids) {
        // remove duplicate dcids and convert to string
        dcids = dcids.filter(function(e, i, ar){ return e.length > 0 && ar.indexOf(e) === i; });
        dcids = dcids.map(Number).join(',');
        return postData({"ac":"buildsel;table=students;list="+dcids});
    }

    // get the current hour in hh24 format and minute
    api.getTimeAndDateInfo = function() {
        var dateInfo = new Date();

        // get time info
        var isAm = (dateInfo.getHours() >= 12);
        var hour = Number(dateInfo.getHours());
        var min = Number(dateInfo.getMinutes());
    
        // get date info
        var dd = dateInfo.getDate();
        var mm = dateInfo.getMonth()+1; // Jan is 0!
        var yyyy = dateInfo.getFullYear();

        // add zeros to months and days
        if(dd<10){ dd='0'+dd };
        if(mm<10){ mm='0'+mm };

        var date = mm+'/'+dd+'/'+yyyy;
        return {date: date, hour: hour, min: min, ampm: (isAm?'am':'pm')};
    }

    //// STORAGE HELPERS
    api.setItem = function(key, data) {
        if(!HAS_LOCALSTORAGE) return null;
        if(typeof data != "string") {
            console.error('api.setItem: data is not a string');
            return
        }
        localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_NAMESPACE+key, data)
    }

    api.getItem = function(key) {
        if(!HAS_LOCALSTORAGE) return null;
        return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_NAMESPACE+key)
    }

    api.setSItem = function(key, data) {
        if(!HAS_LOCALSTORAGE) return null;
        if(typeof data != "string") {
            console.error('api.setItem: data is not a string');
            return
        }
        sessionStorage.setItem(STORAGE_NAMESPACE+key, data)
    }

    api.getSItem = function(key) {
        if(!HAS_LOCALSTORAGE) return null;
        return sessionStorage.getItem(STORAGE_NAMESPACE+key)
    }

    return api

})();

</script>

<script>
var apiStuAlerts = apiStuAlerts || (function() {
	var stuApi = {};
	stuApi.getAlerts = async function(studentid, studcid){
		let schoolID = (0==0) ? 1490080 : 0;
		let types = await apiac.getAlertTypes({disabled: 0,student_schoolid: schoolID});
		let manAlerts = getManualAlerts(types.filter(t => t.trigger_type == 'man'), studentid);
		let sfAlerts = getSFAlerts(types.filter(t => t.trigger_type == 'sf'), studentid);
		let advAlerts = getAdvancedAlerts(types.filter(t => t.trigger_type == 'adv' && t.trigger_url!='QUERY_CHECK.html'), studentid, studcid);
		let allAlerts=[...await manAlerts, ...await sfAlerts, ...await advAlerts];
		let sortedAlerts = await sortAlerts(allAlerts)
		return sortedAlerts;
	};
	async function sortAlerts(arr){
		if(arr.length<0) return Promise.resolve([]);
		try{
			let district = arr.filter(e=>$j(e[0]).attr('school_number')==="0" && $j(e[0]).attr('sort_order') !== "9999999")
							.sort((a,b)=> $j(a[0]).attr('sort_order')-$j(b[0]).attr('sort_order') ||  $j(a[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase().localeCompare($j(b[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase()))
			let school = arr.filter(e=>$j(e[0]).attr('school_number')!=="0" && $j(e[0]).attr('sort_order') !== "9999999")
							.sort((a,b)=> $j(a[0]).attr('sort_order')-$j(b[0]).attr('sort_order') ||  $j(a[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase().localeCompare($j(b[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase()))
			let unsorted = arr.filter(e=>$j(e[0]).attr('sort_order')==="9999999")
							.sort((a,b)=> $j(a[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase().localeCompare($j(b[0]).attr('title').toLowerCase()));
			let sortedArr=[...district,...school,...unsorted];
			return Promise.resolve(sortedArr);
		}
		catch(e){ return Promise.resolve([]); }
	}
	async function getSFAlerts (types, studentid) {
		if(!types.length) return Promise.resolve([]);
		let response = $j.Deferred();
		let sfAlerts = [];

		let fields = [];
		let tables = [];
		types.forEach(function(type){
			let fld = type.student_field.split('.');
			fld = fld.length > 1 ? fld[1] : fld[0];
			let justField = fld;
			fld = type.ext_table_name ? (type.ext_table_name + '.' + fld) : 'students.' + fld;
			if(!fields.includes(fld)) fields.push(`'${justField.toLowerCase()}' VALUE ${fld.toLowerCase()}`);
			if(type.ext_table_name && !tables.includes(type.ext_table_name)) tables.push(type.ext_table_name);
		});

		let select = fields.join (', ');
		let join = '';
		tables.forEach(function(tbl){
			join += ` LEFT JOIN ${tbl} ON ${tbl}.studentsdcid = students.dcid `;
		});

		let params =  {'fields': select, 'joinClause': join, 'stuList': studentid, 'student_id': studentid};
		let url = '/admin/mbaAlerts/api/queries/stuFieldValues.json';
		if('admin' == 'teachers') url = '/teachers/mba_alerts/queries/stuFieldValues.json';
		if('admin' == 'subs') url = '/subs/mba_alerts/queries/stuFieldValues.json';
		if('admin' == 'guardian') url = '/guardian/mba_alerts/queries/stuFieldValues.json';
		
		$j.getJSON(url, params, function(data){
			let fieldVals = data;
			fieldVals.pop();
			types.forEach(function(alert){
				if(alert.trigger_type != 'sf') return;
				let fld = alert.student_field.split('.');
				fld = fld.length > 1 ? fld[1] : fld[0];
				fld = fld.toLowerCase();
				fieldVals.forEach(function(stu){
					let met = false;
					let fieldVal = stu[fld] == null ? '' : String(stu[fld]).toLowerCase();
//					let operand = alert.student_field_operand ? alert.student_field_operand.split(',') : [];
					//handle searches in comma separated list for empty values
					let operand = alert.student_field_operand ? alert.student_field_operand.split(',').map(e=> e.trim()===''? 'iamablankspacebaby' : e.trim().toLowerCase() ) : [];
					if(operand.includes('iamablankspacebaby') && fieldVal==='') fieldVal='iamablankspacebaby';
					if(alert.student_field_operator == 'notblank' && stu[fld]!=null) met = true;
					else if(alert.student_field_operator == 'blank' && stu[fld]==null) met = true;
					else if(alert.student_field_operator == 'notin' && !operand.includes(fieldVal)) met = true;
					else if(alert.student_field_operator == 'in' && operand.includes(fieldVal)) met = true;
					if(met)	sfAlerts.push(apiac.makeAlert({...alert, studentdcid: stu.dcid, studentid: stu.id }));
				});
			});
			response.resolve(sfAlerts);
		});
		return response;
	}

	async function getManualAlerts(types,studentid) {
		if(!types.length) return Promise.resolve([]);
		let manAlerts = [];
		const typeIds = types.map(e => e.id);
		let manualAlerts = await apiac.getAlerts({typeIds: typeIds.join(','), studentIds: studentid});
		manualAlerts.forEach(e => {
			let type = types.filter(k => k.id == e.u_aet_customalerts_typesid)
			if(!type.length) return
			e.type = type[0];
		});

		manualAlerts.forEach(e => {
			if(e.expired || e.inactive) return
			const alert = apiac.makeAlert({
				id: e.id,
				stub_url: e.type.stub_url,
				studentdcid: e.studentsdcid,
				icon_type: e.type.icon_type,
				icon: e.type.icon,
				name: e.type.name,
				color: e.type.color,
				trigger_type: e.type.trigger_type,
				sort_order: e.type.sort_order,
				school_number: e.type.school_number,
				studentid: studentid
			});
			manAlerts.push(alert);
		});
		return Promise.resolve(manAlerts);
	}

	async function getAdvancedAlerts(types, studentid, studcid) {
		let advAlerts = [];
		for (const e of types) {
			let alertInfo = await apiac.getAdvTriggerAlerts({
				trigger_url: e.trigger_url,
				studentIds: studentid,
				frn: `001${studcid}`,
				querystring: e.querystring
			});

			if(alertInfo[studentid]){
				const alert = apiac.makeAlert({
					...e,
					studentid: studentid,
					studentdcid: studcid,
					frn: `001${studcid}`
				});
				advAlerts.push(alert);
			}
		}
		return Promise.resolve(advAlerts);
	}
	return stuApi;
})();
</script>

			let alertTarget=$j('<span>').css('margin-left','5px');
			res.forEach(a =>{ 
			    //newest nav
			    if($j('#student_alerts').length>0){
			        $j('#student_alerts').append($j(a[0]));
			    }
			    else{
					//older versions of PowerSchool
					if($j('#page-heading-alerts').length==0){
						$j('h1').append($j(a[0]));
					}
					else{
						//newer versions of PowerSchool
						if($j('#page-heading-alerts>a').length) {
							let aLength=$j('#page-heading-alerts > a').length;
							$j(a[0]).insertAfter($j('#page-heading-alerts > a:nth-of-type('+aLength+')')[0]);
						}
						else{
							$j("#page-heading-alerts").append($j(a[0]));
						}
					}
				}
			});
		});
	});
